<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:довольство.html>дово́льство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dovólʹstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недовольство.html>недово́льство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedovólʹstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недовольство.html>недово́льства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недовольство.html>недово́льства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недовольство.html>недово́льств</a></b>)

***недоговаривать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недоговаривать.html>недогова́ривать</a> (31312)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">недоговори́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedogovorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоговаривать.html>недогова́ривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedogovárivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">недоговори́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to keep/hold back
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> что́-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоговаривать.html>недогова́ривает</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on štó-to <b>nedogovárivajet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is holding something back</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">недо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">— <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Чего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спрашивать.html>спра́шиваешь</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:приходить.html>приходи́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вздуматься.html>взду́мается</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>вся</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:недолгий.html>недолга́</a></span>! </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недолго.html>недо́лго</a> (3416)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***недолюбливать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недолюбливать.html>недолю́бливать</a> (13958)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">недо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недолюбливать.html>недолю́бливать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedoljúblivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have no special liking/sympathy <i>(for)</i>, to have a dislike <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недолюбливать.html>недолю́бливали</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní drug drúga <b>nedoljúblivali</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there was no love lost between them</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недооценка.html>недооце́нка</a> (32212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недооценить.html>недооцени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedoocenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>недопи́ть</a> (16738)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">недо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>недопи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedopítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">недопива́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to not drink completely</li>
<li>to not drink enough, to not drink until satisfied</li></ol>

***недоразумение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недоразумение.html>недоразуме́ние</a> (7071)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоразумение.html>недоразуме́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedorazuménije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоразумение.html>недоразуме́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоразумение.html>недоразуме́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоразумение.html>недоразуме́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>misunderstanding, misapprehension, misconception</li></ol>

***недоросль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недоросль.html>не́доросль</a> (27961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">недоро́слый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedoróslyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with stress shift typical of the suffix.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоросль.html>не́доросль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nédoroslʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоросль.html>не́доросля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоросль.html>не́доросли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоросль.html>не́дорослей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> adolescent nobleman who has not entered the civil service <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in Russia in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/18th_century" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:18th century">18th century</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ironic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> uneducated, stupid young man</li></ol>

***недоставать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостава́ть</a> (13726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставать.html>достава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dostavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedostavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">недоста́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lack, to be needed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостаёт</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čevó vam <b>nedostajót</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what are you short of?; what are you lacking?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостаёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>nedostajót</b> déneg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is short of money</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостаёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тников</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nam <b>nedostajót</b> rabótnikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we lack workers; we are short of workers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостаёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́в</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выразить.html>вы́разить</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>nedostajót</b> slov, štóby výrazitʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he cannot find words to express</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b>недоста́нет</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>nedostánet</b> sil</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his strength will not suffice him; he will not have sufficient strength</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостава́ло</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo ješčó <b>nedostaválo</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">that's all we needed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to miss
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостава́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вас</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nam óčenʹ <b>nedostaválo</b> vas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we missed you very much; we missed you badly</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́ток</a> (2562)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">недоста́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedostátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́ток</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedostátok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́тка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́тков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lack, deficiency, deficit, shortage</li>
<li>defect, drawback, flaw</li></ol>
